\DoxyCodeLine{00001\ \textcolor{comment}{/**********************************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00002\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00003\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ rlgl\ -\/\ raylib\ OpenGL\ abstraction\ layer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00004\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00005\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ rlgl\ is\ a\ wrapper\ for\ multiple\ OpenGL\ versions\ (1.1,\ 2.1,\ 3.3\ Core,\ ES\ 2.0)\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ pseudo-\/OpenGL\ 1.1\ style\ functions\ (rlVertex,\ rlTranslate,\ rlRotate...).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ When\ chosing\ an\ OpenGL\ version\ greater\ than\ OpenGL\ 1.1,\ rlgl\ stores\ vertex\ data\ on\ internal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ VBO\ buffers\ (and\ VAOs\ if\ available).\ It\ requires\ calling\ 3\ functions:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ rlglInit()\ \ -\/\ Initialize\ internal\ buffers\ and\ auxiliar\ resources}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ rlglDraw()\ \ -\/\ Process\ internal\ buffers\ and\ send\ required\ draw\ calls}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ rlglClose()\ -\/\ De-\/initialize\ internal\ buffers\ data\ and\ other\ auxiliar\ resources}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ CONFIGURATION:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_11}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_21}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_33}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_ES2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Use\ selected\ OpenGL\ graphics\ backend,\ should\ be\ supported\ by\ platform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Those\ preprocessor\ defines\ are\ only\ used\ on\ rlgl\ module,\ if\ OpenGL\ version\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ required\ by\ any\ other\ module,\ use\ rlGetVersion()\ tocheck\ it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RLGL\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Generates\ the\ implementation\ of\ the\ library\ into\ the\ included\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ If\ not\ defined,\ the\ library\ is\ in\ header\ only\ mode\ and\ can\ be\ included\ in\ other\ headers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ or\ source\ files\ without\ problems.\ But\ only\ ONE\ file\ should\ hold\ the\ implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RLGL\_STANDALONE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Use\ rlgl\ as\ standalone\ library\ (no\ raylib\ dependency)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ SUPPORT\_VR\_SIMULATOR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Support\ VR\ simulation\ functionality\ (stereo\ rendering)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ DEPENDENCIES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ raymath\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ 3D\ math\ functionality\ (Vector3,\ Matrix,\ Quaternion)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ GLAD\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ OpenGL\ extensions\ loading\ (OpenGL\ 3.3\ Core\ only)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03624\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ lensRadiusSq\ =\ lensRadius*lensRadius;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03625\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ distortionScale\ =\ hmd.lensDistortionValues[0]\ +}
\DoxyCodeLine{03626\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ hmd.lensDistortionValues[1]*lensRadiusSq\ +}
\DoxyCodeLine{03627\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ hmd.lensDistortionValues[2]*lensRadiusSq*lensRadiusSq\ +}
\DoxyCodeLine{03628\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ hmd.lensDistortionValues[3]*lensRadiusSq*lensRadiusSq*lensRadiusSq;}
